@002B PAD DKAR LTAR BSNGAGS THUGS BSKYED MANDA RA YIS BYA DKA'

BLO GROS GSER BZANG GAR BU NYAMS MYONG BZO BO'I 'DU BYED LAS

GZHON GCIG NYID GANG 'DUL MOS PA'I RDZING BUR DU MAR 'CHAR BA
LAS 'ONGS ZLA MED STON PA RNAM GSUM THUGS

MDANGS DMAR SER 'OD, ,LAM LAM 'BAR BA RAL GRI'I GDENGS KA DANG,

RNAM 'DREN MKHYEN PA'I GTER, ,

BTUNG BAS ZLA ZHAL LANG TSO MA, ,MU TIG 'KHRI SHING RTZE NAS
BEEd'URYA'I, ,DBYID KYI PHO NYA'I GLU YI SHIS BA STZOL, ,SHES
BYA KUN GZIGS MKHYEN PA'I ZLA SHEL MKHYEN

MI SHES ZHES KHENGS BSKYUNGS PA 'BA' ZHIG MDZAD DO, ,DGE BA'I
BSHES GNYEN KHA RGYA'I DAR RGYAS TSANG LA KLONG RDOL BLA MA
